<script>  
(function(){

braze.initialize('c574d66e-2a74-4ef2-b2f0-ae004a66f682', {
  allowUserSuppliedJavascript: true,
  sessionTimeoutInSeconds: 300,
  baseUrl: 'sdk.iad-01.braze.com',
  doNotLoadFontAwesome: true,
  serviceWorkerLocation: '/docs/service-worker.js'
});
braze.subscribeToContentCardsUpdates(function(updates) {
  if (updates.cards.length > 0) {
    $('#cc_prompt').show();
  }
});

braze.automaticallyShowInAppMessages();

try {
  if (window.localStorage.getItem('braze_developer_data')) {
    const developerData = JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem('braze_developer_data'));
    if (developerData.id) {
      window.localStorage.setItem('braze_external_id', developerData.id);
      braze.changeUser(developerData.id);
      if (developerData.email) {
        braze.getUser().setEmail(developerData.email);
      }
      ['department', 'companyId', 'companyName', 'username', 'env', 'industry', 'locale', 'dashboard', 'appGroupId'].forEach(attribute => {
        if (developerData[attribute]) {
          braze.getUser().setCustomUserAttribute(attribute, developerData[attribute]);
        }
      });
    }
    window.localStorage.removeItem('braze_developer_data');
  }
} catch (e) {
  console.error('Error setting user ID:', e);
}


braze.openSession();
if (braze.getCachedContentCards()?.cards?.length > 0) {
  $('#cc_prompt').show();
} else {
  braze.requestContentCardsRefresh();
}

var [, base, ...paths] = window.location.pathname.split('/');
if (base === 'docs'){
  braze.logCustomEvent( 'docs_page', {
    url: window.location.href,
    section: paths.join('/'),
    hash: window.location.hash,
    anchor: window.location.hash.split('?')[0]
  });
  braze.requestImmediateDataFlush();
}

})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

  function removeleadingslash(str){
    var rstr = str;
    if (rstr.slice(-1) === "/") {
      rstr = rstr.slice(0, -1);
    }
    return rstr;
  }

var validurls = (typeof validurls === "undefined")  ? {} : validurls;

// multi language broken link redirects
if (site_language && (site_language != 'en')){
  var base_url = '/docs';
  for (var url in validurls) {
    var adjusted_url = url;
    var adjusted_destination = (Array.isArray(validurls[url]) ? validurls[url][0] : validurls[url]) || "";
    if (!adjusted_url.match(/^\/docs\/(\w{2}|\w{2}\-\w{2})\//)) {
      adjusted_url = adjusted_url.replace(/^\/docs\//, `\/docs\/${site_language}\/`);
    }
    if (!adjusted_destination.match(/^\/docs\/(\w{2}|\w{2}\-\w{2})\//)) {
      adjusted_destination = adjusted_destination.replace(/^\/docs\//, `\/docs\/${site_language}\/`);
    }
    validurls[adjusted_url] = adjusted_destination;
  };
}

(function(){
  //lower case name => path name

  var urlpath = removeleadingslash(window.location.pathname);

  var pagetype = urlpath.split('/');
  function redirecturl(ky,uh,redirect) {
    var val_urls = validurls[ky];
    var hashes = val_urls.split('#');
    var redirect_params = ((hashes[0].indexOf('?') > -1 ) ? '&' : '?') + redirect;
    var returl = hashes[0] + redirect_params;

    if (hashes[1]) {
      returl += '#' + hashes[1];
    }
    else if (uh ) {
      returl += uh;
    }
    return returl;
  }

  var siteurl = '';
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/home/home/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/admin_settings/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/admin_settings/contact_information/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/admin_settings/notification_preferences/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/admin_settings/security_settings/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/admin_settings/security_settings/security_export_s3/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/admin_settings/workspace_time_zone/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/billing/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/billing/message_usage_dashboard/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/create_and_manage_workspaces/");
    validurls['/docs' + siteurl.toLowerCase()] = '/docs' + siteurl + '/';
    
    siteurl = removeleadingslash("/user_guide/administer/global/privacy/");

    var urlhash = window.location.hash;
  var urlsearch = window.location.search;

  var redirected_count = parseInt(query_params.get('redirected'),10) || 0;

  if (redirected_count < max_redirects) {
    redirected_count++
    query_params.set('redirected',redirected_count );
    redirected = query_params.toString();

    if (validurls[urlpath.toLowerCase() + '/' + urlhash] ) {
      return location.href = redirecturl(urlpath.toLowerCase() + '/' + urlhash,urlhash,redirected);
    }
    else if (validurls[urlpath.toLowerCase() + urlhash] ) {
      return location.href = redirecturl(urlpath.toLowerCase() + urlhash,urlhash,redirected);
    }
    else if (validurls[urlpath.toLowerCase() + '/'] ) {
      return location.href = redirecturl(urlpath.toLowerCase() + '/',urlhash,redirected);
    }
    else if (validurls[urlpath.toLowerCase()] ) {
      return location.href = redirecturl(urlpath.toLowerCase(),urlhash,redirected);
    }
    else if (urlpath.match(/\/docs\/(\w{2}|\w{2}\-\w{2})\//)){
      return location.href = urlpath.toLowerCase().replace(/\/docs\/(\w{2}|\w{2}\-\w{2})\//,"/docs/");
    }
  }

  window.braze.logCustomEvent("broken page", {
    hostname: location.hostname,
    pathname: location.pathname,
  });
  window.braze.requestImmediateDataFlush();
})();

$(document).ready(function(k){
  var search_strings = removeleadingslash(window.location.pathname).split('/');
  var search_string = search_strings[search_strings.length -1].replace(/(\W|_|-)+/g,' ');
  var urlhash = window.location.hash;
  if (urlhash) {
      search_string += ' ' + urlhash.replace(/(\W|_|-)+/g,' ');
  }
  $('#help-menu_search').val(search_string)
});
</script>

 </a>
 <div id="contentcards">
 </div>

<style>
.ask-ai-inline {
  position: relative;
  display: inline-flex;
  flex: 0 0 auto;
  max-width: 100%;
}
.ask-ai-inline-btn {
  display: inline-flex;
  align-items: center;
  gap: 0.5rem;
  font-size: 0.875rem;
  padding: 0.375rem 0.75rem;
  border: 1px solid #801ED7;
  background-color: transparent;
  color: #801ED7;
  border-radius: 0.375rem;
  transition: all 0.15s ease-in-out;
  cursor: pointer;
  box-shadow: none;
  text-decoration: none;
  font-family: inherit;
  line-height: 1.5;
}
.ask-ai-inline-btn:hover {
  background-color: #801ED7;
  color: white;
  border-color: #801ED7;
  box-shadow: none;
  text-decoration: none;
}
.ask-ai-inline-btn:focus {
  outline: 0;
  box-shadow: 0 0 0 0.2rem rgba(128, 30, 215, 0.25);
}
.ask-ai-inline-chevron {
  width: 10px;
  height: 10px;
  flex-shrink: 0;
  transition: transform 0.15s;
}
.ask-ai-inline.open .ask-ai-inline-chevron {
  transform: rotate(180deg);
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown {
  display: none;
  position: absolute;
  top: calc(100% + 4px);
  left: 0;
  min-width: 200px;
  max-width: min(280px, calc(100vw - 24px));
  background: #fff;
  border: 1px solid #e5e7eb;
  border-radius: 8px;
  box-shadow: 0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.10);
  z-index: 1000;
  overflow: hidden;
}
.ask-ai-inline.open .ask-ai-inline-dropdown {
  display: block;
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option,
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:link,
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:visited,
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:hover,
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:active,
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:focus {
  display: flex !important;
  align-items: center !important;
  gap: 12px !important;
  padding: 12px 16px !important;
  color: #1f2937 !important;
  text-decoration: none !important;
  font-size: 0.875rem !important;
  font-family: inherit !important;
  font-weight: 500 !important;
  white-space: nowrap !important;
  border: none !important;
  border-bottom: 1px solid #f3f4f6 !important;
  border-width: 0 0 1px 0 !important;
  border-color: #f3f4f6 !important;
  background-color: transparent !important;
  box-shadow: none !important;
  outline: none !important;
  transition: background 0.12s !important;
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:last-child,
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:last-child:hover {
  border-bottom: none !important;
  border-width: 0 !important;
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:hover {
  background-color: #f9fafb !important;
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown a.ask-ai-inline-option:focus-visible {
  outline: 2px solid #801ED7 !important;
  outline-offset: -2px !important;
  background-color: #f9fafb !important;
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown .fa-external-link-alt {
  display: none !important;
}
.ask-ai-inline-dropdown .inline-link {
  display: contents !important;
}
.ask-ai-inline-option-icon {
  width: 18px;
  height: 18px;
  flex-shrink: 0;
}
.ask-ai-inline-option-name {
  flex: 1;
  font-weight: 500;
}
@media (max-width: 768px) {
  .ask-ai-inline-btn {
    font-size: 0.8rem;
    padding: 0.3rem 0.6rem;
  }

  .ask-ai-inline-dropdown {
    left: auto;
    right: 0;
  }
}

@media print {
  .ask-ai-inline {
    display: none;
  }
}
</style>

<script>
(function() {
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    function getMarkdownPath(pathname) {
      if (!pathname) {
        return '/index.md';
      }

      if (pathname.endsWith('/index.md')) {
        return pathname;
      }

      if (pathname.endsWith('/')) {
        return pathname.slice(0, -1) + '/index.md';
      }

      if (pathname.endsWith('.html')) {
        return pathname.replace('.html', '/index.md');
      }

      return pathname + '/index.md';
    }

    function logAskAiEvent(eventName, properties) {
      if (!window.braze?.logCustomEvent) {
        return;
      }

      braze.logCustomEvent(eventName, properties);
      braze.requestImmediateDataFlush();
    }

    var markdownPath = getMarkdownPath(window.location.pathname);
    var pageUrl = window.location.origin + markdownPath;

    var claudePrompt = 'Hi Claude! Can you please read ' + pageUrl + ' and prepare to answer questions about it?';
    var chatgptPrompt = 'Hi ChatGPT! Can you please read ' + pageUrl + ' and prepare to answer questions about it?';

    var claudeUrl = 'https://claude.ai/new?q=' + encodeURIComponent(claudePrompt);
    var chatgptUrl = 'https://chatgpt.com/?model=auto&q=' + encodeURIComponent(chatgptPrompt);

    var dropdownId = 'ask-ai-dropdown-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);

    var wrapper = document.createElement('div');
    wrapper.className = 'ask-ai-inline';
    wrapper.innerHTML =
      '<button class="ask-ai-inline-btn" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="menu" aria-controls="' + dropdownId + '">' +
        '<i class="fas fa-magic" aria-hidden="true"></i>' +
        '<span>Ask AI</span>' +
        '<svg class="ask-ai-inline-chevron" viewBox="0 0 10 10" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true">' +
          '<path d="M2 3.5L5 6.5L8 3.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/>' +
        '</svg>' +
      '</button>' +
      '<div id="' + dropdownId + '" class="ask-ai-inline-dropdown" role="menu" aria-label="Ask AI options">' +
        '<a class="ask-ai-inline-option extignore" role="menuitem" tabindex="-1" data-ai-option="claude" href="' + claudeUrl + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">' +
          '<svg class="ask-ai-inline-option-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true">' +
            '<path d="M12 2V8.5M12 22V15.5M2 12H8.5M22 12H15.5M4.93 4.93L9.17 9.17M19.07 19.07L14.83 14.83M4.93 19.07L9.17 14.83M19.07 4.93L14.83 9.17" stroke="#D97757" stroke-width="2.2" stroke-linecap="round"/>' +
          '</svg>' +
          '<span class="ask-ai-inline-option-name">Claude</span>' +
          '<span class="sr-only"> (opens in new tab)</span>' +
        '</a>' +
        '<a class="ask-ai-inline-option extignore" role="menuitem" tabindex="-1" data-ai-option="chatgpt" href="' + chatgptUrl + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">' +
          '<svg class="ask-ai-inline-option-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true">' +
            '<path d="M22.282 9.821a5.985 5.985 0 0 0-.516-4.91 6.046 6.046 0 0 0-6.51-2.9A6.065 6.065 0 0 0 4.981 4.18a5.998 5.998 0 0 0-3.998 2.9 6.046 6.046 0 0 0 .743 7.097 5.98 5.98 0 0 0 .51 4.911 6.051 6.051 0 0 0 6.516 2.9A5.985 5.985 0 0 0 13.26 24a6.056 6.056 0 0 0 5.772-4.206 5.99 5.99 0 0 0 3.997-2.9 6.056 6.056 0 0 0-.747-7.073zM13.26 22.43a4.476 4.476 0 0 1-2.876-1.04l.141-.081 4.779-2.758a.795.795 0 0 0 .392-.681v-6.737l2.02 1.168a.071.071 0 0 1 .038.052v5.583a4.504 4.504 0 0 1-4.494 4.494zM3.6 18.304a4.47 4.47 0 0 1-.535-3.014l.142.085 4.783 2.759a.771.771 0 0 0 .78 0l5.843-3.369v2.332a.08.08 0 0 1-.033.062L9.74 19.95a4.5 4.5 0 0 1-6.14-1.646zM2.34 7.896a4.485 4.485 0 0 1 2.366-1.973V11.6a.766.766 0 0 0 .388.676l5.815 3.355-2.02 1.168a.076.076 0 0 1-.071 0l-4.83-2.786A4.504 4.504 0 0 1 2.34 7.872v.024zm16.597 3.855l-5.833-3.387L15.119 7.2a.076.076 0 0 1 .071 0l4.83 2.791a4.494 4.494 0 0 1-.676 8.105v-5.678a.79.79 0 0 0-.407-.667zm2.01-3.023l-.141-.085-4.774-2.782a.776.776 0 0 0-.785 0L9.409 9.23V6.897a.066.066 0 0 1 .028-.061l4.83-2.787a4.5 4.5 0 0 1 6.68 4.66v.018zm-12.64 4.135l-2.02-1.164a.08.08 0 0 1-.038-.057V6.075a4.5 4.5 0 0 1 7.375-3.453l-.142.08L8.704 5.46a.795.795 0 0 0-.393.681l-.004 6.722zm1.097-2.365l2.602-1.5 2.602 1.5v3.001l-2.602 1.5-2.602-1.5V10.5z" fill="#10a37f"/>' +
          '</svg>' +
          '<span class="ask-ai-inline-option-name">ChatGPT</span>' +
          '<span class="sr-only"> (opens in new tab)</span>' +
        '</a>' +
        '<a class="ask-ai-inline-option extignore" role="menuitem" tabindex="-1" data-ai-option="docs_mcp" href="https://www.braze.com/docs/developer_guide/getting_started/build_with_llm" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">' +
          '<svg class="ask-ai-inline-option-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true">' +
            '<path d="M4 6h16M4 12h16M4 18h10" stroke="#6b7280" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"/>' +
            '<circle cx="20" cy="18" r="2.5" stroke="#6b7280" stroke-width="1.5" fill="none"/>' +
            '<path d="M22 20l1.5 1.5" stroke="#6b7280" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round"/>' +
          '</svg>' +
          '<span class="ask-ai-inline-option-name">Docs MCP</span>' +
          '<span class="sr-only"> (opens in new tab)</span>' +
        '</a>' +
      '</div>';

    var llmWrapper = document.querySelector('.copy-for-llm-wrapper');
    if (llmWrapper) {
      llmWrapper.appendChild(wrapper);
    } else {
      var container = document.createElement('div');
      container.className = 'copy-for-llm-page-header';
      var innerWrapper = document.createElement('div');
      innerWrapper.className = 'copy-for-llm-wrapper';
      innerWrapper.appendChild(wrapper);
      container.appendChild(innerWrapper);

      var firstH1 = document.querySelector('#article-main h1');
      if (firstH1) {
        firstH1.parentNode.insertBefore(container, firstH1.nextSibling);
      }
    }

    setTimeout(function() {
      wrapper.querySelectorAll('.fa-external-link-alt').forEach(function(icon) {
        icon.remove();
      });
      wrapper.querySelectorAll('.inline-link').forEach(function(span) {
        while (span.firstChild) {
          span.parentNode.insertBefore(span.firstChild, span);
        }
        span.remove();
      });
    }, 0);

    var btn = wrapper.querySelector('.ask-ai-inline-btn');
    var dropdown = wrapper.querySelector('.ask-ai-inline-dropdown');

    function positionDropdown() {
      if (!dropdown) return;

      dropdown.style.left = '0';
      dropdown.style.right = 'auto';

      var rect = dropdown.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (rect.right > window.innerWidth - 8) {
        dropdown.style.left = 'auto';
        dropdown.style.right = '0';
      }

      rect = dropdown.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (rect.left < 8) {
        dropdown.style.left = '0';
        dropdown.style.right = 'auto';
      }
    }

    function getMenuItems() {
      return Array.from(dropdown.querySelectorAll('[role="menuitem"]'));
    }

    function openMenu() {
      wrapper.classList.add('open');
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
      positionDropdown();
      var items = getMenuItems();
      if (items.length) items[0].focus();
      logAskAiEvent("ask_ai_menu_opened", {
        page_url: window.location.pathname,
        page_title: document.title,
        markdown_url: markdownPath
      });
    }

    function closeMenu(returnFocus) {
      wrapper.classList.remove('open');
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
      if (returnFocus) btn.focus();
    }

    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
      wrapper.classList.contains('open') ? closeMenu(false) : openMenu();
    });

    btn.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'ArrowDown' || e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
        e.preventDefault();
        openMenu();
      }
    });

    dropdown.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      var items = getMenuItems();
      var idx = items.indexOf(document.activeElement);

      switch (e.key) {
        case 'ArrowDown':
          e.preventDefault();
          items[(idx + 1) % items.length].focus();
          break;
        case 'ArrowUp':
          e.preventDefault();
          items[(idx - 1 + items.length) % items.length].focus();
          break;
        case 'Home':
          e.preventDefault();
          items[0].focus();
          break;
        case 'End':
          e.preventDefault();
          items[items.length - 1].focus();
          break;
        case 'Escape':
          e.preventDefault();
          closeMenu(true);
          break;
        case 'Tab':
          closeMenu(false);
          break;
      }
    });

    wrapper.querySelectorAll('.ask-ai-inline-option').forEach(function(option) {
      option.addEventListener('click', function() {
        var optionValue = option.getAttribute('data-ai-option') || 'unknown';
        var baseOptionProperties = {
          page_url: window.location.pathname,
          page_title: document.title,
          markdown_url: markdownPath,
          option: optionValue,
          option_name: optionValue,
          target_url: option.getAttribute('href') || ''
        };
        logAskAiEvent("ask_ai_option_clicked", baseOptionProperties);

        if (["chatgpt", "claude", "docs_mcp"].includes(optionValue)) {
          logAskAiEvent("ask_ai_option_clicked_" + optionValue, baseOptionProperties);
        }
      });
    });

    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      if (!wrapper.contains(e.target)) {
        closeMenu(false);
      }
    });

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Escape' && wrapper.classList.contains('open')) {
        closeMenu(true);
      }
    });

    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
      if (wrapper.classList.contains('open')) {
        positionDropdown();
      }
    });
  });
})();
</script>




</main>
</body>
</html>
